Sub-agents: ingest, auditor, fixer, reporter.\n- `seo/detector.py` = deterministic detectors (extend to the full rulebook — biggest score).\n- `mcp/server.py` = MCP tools + the live dashboard.\n\n## Conventions\n- Commit after each working step with a real message.\n- Run `python run.py sample-export/` to test end to end.\n\n## Things I have learned during the build\n\n- Screaming Frog leaves Title 1 blank on redirect and non-HTML rows — always filter\n  `is_html(r) and is_200(r)` before any title/meta check, or counts inflate.\n- `indexable(r)` checks `Indexability == \"Indexable\"` (case-sensitive strip). Non-indexable\n  pages must be excluded from missing/duplicate title and meta checks per rulebook.\n- `redirect_chain` requires a pre-built set of all 3xx Address values. Then for each 3xx\n  row, check if its Redirect URL is in that set. Do NOT just check status code of target.\n- `duplicate_*` detectors: build a dict of value → [urls], then flag entries with len > 1.\n  Only use indexable pages as inputs to avoid noise from redirected/canonicalised pages.\n- Dashboard (localhost:7700) was not loading because run.py was not starting mcp/server.py\n  as a subprocess first. Quality only — it does not hunt for bugs; use /code-review for that.\n- fewer-permission-prompts: Scan your transcripts for common read-only Bash and MCP tool calls, then add a prioritized allowlist to project .claude/settings.json to reduce permission prompts.\n- loop: Run a prompt or slash command on a recurring interval (e.g. /loop 5m /foo). Omit the interval to let the model self-pace. - When the user wants to set up a recurring task, poll for status, or run something repeatedly on an interval (e.g. \"check the deploy every 5 minutes\", \"keep running /babysit-prs\"). Do NOT invoke for one-off tasks.\n- schedule: Create, update, list, or run scheduled remote agents (routines) that execute on a cron schedule. - When the user wants to schedule a recurring remote agent, set up automated tasks, create a cron job for Claude Code, or manage their scheduled agents/routines. Also use when the user wants a one-time scheduled run (\"run this once at 3pm\", \"remind me to check X tomorrow\").\n- claude-api: Reference for the Claude API / Anthropic SDK — model ids, pricing, params, streaming, tool use, MCP, agents, caching, token counting, model migration.\nTRIGGER — read BEFORE opening the target file; don't skip because it \"looks like a one-liner\" — whenever: the prompt names Claude/Anthropic in any form (Claude, Anthropic, Opus, Sonnet, Haiku, `anthropic`, `@anthropic-ai`, `claude-*`, `us.anthropic.*`, `[1m]`); the user asks about an LLM (pricing/model choice/limits/caching) — never answer from memory; OR the task is LLM-shaped with provider unstated (agent/MCP/tool-definition/multi-agent/RAG/LLM-judge/computer-use; generate/summarize/extract/classify/rewrite/converse over NL; debugging refusals/cutoffs/streaming/tool-calls/tokens).\nSKIP only when another provider is being worked on (overrides all triggers): OpenAI/GPT/Gemini/Llama/Mistral/Cohere/Ollama named in the query; OR `grep -rE 'openai|langchain_openai|google.generativeai|genai|mistralai|cohere|ollama'` over the project hits (run this grep FIRST if no provider named — don't Read the file).\n- run: Launch and drive this project's app to see a change working. Use when asked to run, start, or screenshot the app, or to confirm a change works in the real app (not just tests). First looks for a project skill that already covers launching the app; otherwise falls back to built-in patterns per project type (CLI, server, TUI, Electron, browser-driven, library).\n- init: Initialize a new CLAUDE.md file with codebase documentation\n- review: Review a pull request\n- security-review: Complete a security review of the pending changes on the current branch","skillCount":13,"isInitial":true,"names":["update-config","keybindings-help","verify","code-review","simplify","fewer-permission-prompts","loop","schedule","claude-api","run","init","review","security-review"]},"type":"attachment","uuid":"09031d06-37c0-4e18-bdfc-2561ffde515f","timestamp":"2026-06-06T11:04:52.315Z","userType":"external","entrypoint":"cli","cwd":"C:\\Users\\bisht\\Forge-Claude Code\\forge-sprint-01-starter","sessionId":"4afcadad-9b94-452c-8921-7b2f14063d33","version":"2.1.167","gitBranch":"HEAD","slug":"melodic-painting-garden"}

This is YOUR file.\n\n## What we are building\nA Claude Code plugin that ingests a Screaming Frog SEO export (`internal_all.csv` + issue\nCSVs), audits it against the rulebook, prioritizes issues, writes fixes, serves a live\ndashboard at localhost:7700, and outputs `outputs/report.json` + `outputs/report.html`.\n\n## Hard rules (the agent must follow these)\n- Detect issues in **plain Python** (csv/pandas). Use the model only for judgment\n  (rewriting titles/metas, choosing redirect targets). Never feed raw crawl rows to the model.\n- `outputs/report.json` MUST match `report.schema.json`. Validate before declaring done.\n- Filter to `text/html` + indexable pages before title/meta checks (see `rulebook.md`).\n- Do not hard-code anything to the sample export — it must work on an unseen export.\n- Keep model calls small and few (free-tier quota). One page per fix call.\n\n## Architecture (keep it real)\n- `skills/seo-audit/SKILL.md` orchestrates. Sub-agents: ingest, auditor, fixer, reporter.\n- `seo/detector.py` = deterministic detectors (extend to the full rulebook — biggest score).\n- `mcp/server.py` = MCP tools + the live dashboard.\n\n## Conventions\n- Commit after each working step with a real message.\n- Run `python run.py sample-export/` to test end to end.\n## Things I have learned during the build\n\n- Screaming Frog leaves Title 1 blank on redirect and non-HTML rows — always filter\n  `is_html(r) and is_200(r)` before any title/meta check, or counts inflate.\n- `indexable(r)` checks `Indexability == \"Indexable\"` (case-sensitive strip). Non-indexable\n  pages must be excluded from missing/duplicate title and meta checks per rulebook.\n- `redirect_chain` requires a pre-built set of all 3xx Address values. Then for each 3xx\n  row, check if its Redirect URL is in that set. Do NOT just check status code of target.\n- `duplicate_*` detectors: build a dict of value → [urls], then flag entries with len > 1.\n  Only use indexable pages as inputs to avoid noise from redirected/canonicalised pages.\n- Rulebook has no status code restriction on `slow_page` or `non_indexable_but_linked`.\n  Never add is_200() unless the rulebook explicitly requires it.\n- Dashboard SSE fix required two separate things: (1) emit_fn callback pattern so each\n  detector fires _emit immediately rather than batch-emitting after detect() returns,\n  (2) keepalive loop at end of run.py so the daemon thread HTTP server stays alive\n  after the audit completes — without it, ERR_CONNECTION_REFUSED on every browser load.\n- Parallel subagents on files that share a function signature cause merge collisions and\n  worktree creation. Always use one sequential agent for cross-file changes.\n- `Response Time` column uses floats — always use `_float()` not `_int()`.\n- `Word Count` can be empty string in some rows — `_int()` handles None/empty safely.\n- 12/17 detectors fire on sample export — 5 return zero hits because the sample dataset\n  lacks those conditions. --- Response codes ---\n    add(\"broken_link\", \"High\",\n        [r[\"Address\"] for r in rows if 400 <= _int(r.get(\"Status Code\")) <= 499],\n        \"URLs returning a client error (4xx).\")\n    add(\"server_error\", \"High\",\n        [r[\"Address\"] for r in rows if 500 <= _int(r.get(\"Status Code\")) <= 599],\n        \"URLs returning a server error (5xx).\")\n    add(\"redirect\", \"Medium\",\n        [r[\"Address\"] for r in rows if 300 <= _int(r.get(\"Status Code\")) <= 399],\n        \"URLs that redirect (3xx).\")\n\n    # --- Orphan pages ---\n    add(\"orphan_page\", \"Medium\",\n        [r[\"Address\"] for r in idx200 if _int(r.get(\"Inlinks\")) == 0],\n        \"Indexable pages with zero internal links in.\")\n\n    # --- Meta Descriptions ---\n    add(\"missing_meta_description\", \"Medium\",\n        [r[\"Address\"] for r in idx200 if not (r.get(\"Meta Description 1\", \"\") or \"\").strip()],\n        \"Indexable pages missing a meta description.\")\n\n    by_meta = defaultdict(list)\n    for r in idx200:\n        m = (r.get(\"Meta Description 1\", \"\") or \"\").strip()\n        if m:\n            by_meta[m].append(r[\"Address\"])\n    dup_m = [u for urls in by_meta.values() if len(urls) > 1 for u in urls]\n    add(\"duplicate_meta_description\", \"Medium\", dup_m, \"Pages sharing an identical meta description.\")\n\n    add(\"meta_description_too_long\", \"Low\",\n        [r[\"Address\"] for r in idx200 if _int(r.get(\"Meta Description 1 Length\")) > 155],\n        \"Meta descriptions that are likely truncated.\")\n\n    # --- Headings ---\n    add(\"missing_h1\", \"Medium\",\n        [r[\"Address\"] for r in html if is_200(r) and not (r.get(\"H1-1\", \"\") or \"\").strip()],\n        \"200 OK HTML pages missing an H1 tag.\")\n\n    by_h1 = defaultdict(list)\n    for r in idx200:\n        h1 = (r.get(\"H1-1\", \"\") or \"\").strip()\n        if h1:\n            by_h1[h1].append(r[\"Address\"])\n    dup_h1 = [u for urls in by_h1.values() if len(urls) > 1 for u in urls]\n    add(\"duplicate_h1\", \"Low\", dup_h1, \"Indexable pages sharing an identical H1.\")\n\n    # --- Content & Performance ---\n    add(\"title_too_short\", \"Low\",\n        [r[\"Address\"] for r in idx200 if _int(r.get(\"Title 1 Length\")) < 30 and (r.get(\"Title 1\", \"\") or \"\").strip()],\n        \"Titles that are too short to be effective.\")\n\n    add(\"thin_content\", \"Low\",\n        [r[\"Address\"] for r in idx200 if _int(r.get(\"Word Count\")) < 200],\n        \"Indexable pages with very low word count.\")\n\n    add(\"non_indexable_but_linked\", \"Medium\",\n        [r[\"Address\"] for r in html if is_200(r) and not indexable(r) and _int(r.get(\"Inlinks\")) > 0],\n        \"Non-indexable pages that are still being linked to.\")\n\n    add(\"slow_page\", \"Low\",\n        [r[\"Address\"] for r in html if is_200(r) and _float(r.get(\"Response Time\")) > 1.0],\n        \"Pages with a response time greater than 1 second.\")\n\n    # --- Chains ---\n    redirects_3xx = {r[\"Address\"] for r in rows if 300 <= _int(r.get(\"Status Code\")) <= 399}\n    chains = [r[\"Address\"] for r in rows if 300 <= _int(r.get(\"Status Code\")) <= 399 and r.get(\"Redirect URL\") in redirects_3xx]\n    add(\"redirect_chain\", \"High\", chains, \"Redirects that lead to another redirect.\")\n\n    return issues\n\n\ndef summarize(issues: list[dict]) -> dict:\n    by_sev = defaultdict(int)\n    for i in issues:\n        by_sev[i[\"severity\"]] += 1\n    return {\"total_issues\": len(issues),\n            \"by_severity\": {\"High\": by_sev[\"High\"], \"Medium\": by_sev[\"Medium\"], \"Low\": by_sev[\"Low\"]}}\n\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    import sys, json\n    d = sys.argv[1] if len(sys.argv) > 1 else \"../sample-export\"\n    rows = load_rows(d)\n    iss = detect(rows)\n    print(f\"Loaded {len(rows)} rows, detected {len(iss)} issue types.\")\n    print(json.dumps(summarize(iss), indent=2))\n    for i in iss:\n        print(f\"  [{i['severity']:<6}] {i['type']:<24} x{i['count']}\")\n","numLines":164,"startLine":1,"totalLines":164}},"sourceToolAssistantUUID":"4baa2d74-c3a3-4532-84ff-c236868d03a5","sessionKind":"bg","userType":"external","entrypoint":"cli","cwd":"C:\\Users\\bisht\\Forge-Claude Code\\forge-sprint-01-starter","sessionId":"72889e48-e4af-4dbd-b9ed-e5fed8e6c59a","version":"2.1.167","gitBranch":"HEAD"}

The page will still be crawled (to see the directive), but it will then be dropped from the index.\",\"URLs with a 'none' should be reviewed carefully to ensure they are correct and shouldn't be indexed. If these pages should be indexed, then the 'none' directive should be removed.\",\"\"\n47\t\"H2: Multiple\",\"Warning\",\"Low\",\"65\",\"58.560\",\"Pages which have multiple <h2>s. This is not an issue as HTML standards allow multiple <h2>'s when used in a logical hierarchical heading structure. However, this filter can help you quickly scan to review if they are used appropriately.\",\"Ensure <h2>s are used in a logical hierarchical heading structure, and update where appropriate utilising the full heading rank between (h3 - h6) for additional headings.\",\"\"\n48\t\"Pagination: Sequence Error\",\"Issue\",\"Low\",\"1\",\"0.900\",\"URLs that have an error in the rel=\"\"next\"\" and rel=\"\"prev\"\" HTML link elements sequence. This check ensures that URLs contained within rel=\"\"next\"\" and rel=\"\"prev\"\" HTML link elements reciprocate and confirm their relationship in the series.\",\"Ensure paginated URLs contained within rel=\"\"next\"\" or rel=\"\"prev\"\" attributes and within <a> tags are to the correct pages in the sequence.\",\"\"\n49\t\"URL: Over 115 Characters\",\"Opportunity\",\"Low\",\"8\",\"1.750\",\"URLs that are more than the configured length. This is generally not an issue, however research has shown that users prefer shorter, concise URL strings.\",\"Where possible use logical and concise URLs for users and search engines. However, changing URLs is a big decision, and often it's not worth changing them for SEO purposes alone. If URLs are changed, then appropriate 301 redirects must be implemented.\",\"\"\n50\t"}]},"uuid":"18d9f1a6-911f-4e83-86b9-acdfd6341692","timestamp":"2026-06-06T08:26:29.677Z","toolUseResult":{"type":"text","file":{"filePath":"C:\\Users\\bisht\\Forge-Claude Code\\forge-sprint-01-starter\\sample-export\\issues_reports\\issues_overview_report.csv","content":"\"Issue Name\",\"Issue Type\",\"Issue Priority\",\"URLs\",\"% of Total\",\"Description\",\"How To Fix\",\"Help URL\"\n\"H1: Non-Sequential\",\"Warning\",\"Low\",\"1\",\"0.900\",\"Pages with an <h1> that is not the first heading on the page. It helps save developers time from having to specify the protocol and lets the browser determine it based upon the current connection to the resource. However, this technique is now an anti-pattern with HTTPS everywhere, and can expose some sites to 'man in the middle' compromises and performance issues\",\"Update any resource links to be absolute links including the scheme (HTTPS) to avoid security and performance issues.\",\"\"\n\"URL: Non ASCII Characters\",\"Warning\",\"Low\",\"2\",\"0.440\",\"URLs with characters outside of the ASCII character-set. Today browsers and the search engines are largely able to transform URLs accurately.\",\"\"\n\"Response Codes: External Client Error (4xx)\",\"Warning\",\"Low\",\"4\",\"0.800\",\"External URLs with a client-side error. A 404 'Page Not Found' is the most common, and often referred to as a broken link. calling `seo_set_fixes`.\n- `reporter.md`: Creating the final report synthesis and calling `seo_report` and `seo_export`.\n\n**MCP Server Responsibilities**:\n- **Tool Exposure**: Exposes `load`, `detect_issues`, `set_fixes`, `recommend`, `write_report`, and `export_report` as MCP tools.\n- **State Management**: Maintains the `RUN` dictionary as the global state for the current session.\n- **Dashboard Hosting**: Serves `index.html` and `app.js`, and provides a `/state` endpoint for a snapshot and an `/events` endpoint (SSE) for real-time updates.\n- **Event Emission**: Uses `_emit` to push events (`loaded`, `issue`, `summary`, `fixes`, `recommendations`, `saved`, `exported`) to connected dashboard clients.\n- **HTML Generation**: Renders the final HTML report via `_render_html`.\n\n**Dashboard Event Flow**:\n- Dashboard connects to `/events` (SSE).\n- Server pushes JSON payloads: `{\"event\": \"...\", \"data\": ...}`.\n- `seo_load` $\\to$ `loaded` event.\n- `seo_export` $\\to$ `exported` event.\n\n**Report Generation Flow**:\n1.  `seo_report()`:\n    - Collects `site`, `urls_crawled`, `summary`, `issues`, `fixes`, `recommendations`, and `run_meta`.\n    - Writes this object to `outputs/report.json`.\n2.  `seo_export()`:\n    - Takes the same report object.\n    - Renders it into a stylized HTML page via `_render_html`.\n    - Writes the result to `outputs/report.html`.\n\n**Detector Flow**:\n1.  `seo_load` $\\to$ `detector.load_rows(export_dir)` (reads CSVs).\n2.  `seo_detect` $\\to$ `detector.detect(rows)` $\\to$ calls individual rulebook detectors $\\to$ returns a list of issues.\n3.  `seo_detect` also calls `detector.summarize(issues)` to calculate totals and severity counts.\n\n**TODO Locations**:\n- `run.py`: Lines 12-13 mention Schema for the final report.json\n├── rulebook.md                 # The SEO rules the detectors implement\n└── seo-command-center/\n    ├── run.py                  # Headless runner for the full pipeline\n    ├── agents/                  # AI Agent definitions\n    │   ├── auditor.md           # Prioritizes and analyzes issues\n    │   ├── fixer.md             # Generates content fixes\n    │   ├── ingest.md            # Handles data loading and cleaning\n    │   └── reporter.md         # Synthesizes the final report\n    ├── commands/               # Defined commands for Claude Code\n    │   └── seo-audit.md\n    ├── dashboard/               # Live dashboard frontend\n    │   ├── app.js               # Frontend logic & SSE handling\n    │   └── index.html            # Dashboard UI\n    ├── mcp/                     # MCP Server & Pipeline Coordination\n    │   └── server.py            # Core state management & tool exposure\n    ├── outputs/                 # Generated audit results\n    │   ├── report.json          # Structured audit data\n    │   └── report.html          # Client-facing HTML report\n    ├── seo/                     # Deterministic detection logic\n    │   └── detector.py           # Rulebook implementation (CSV processing)\n    └── skills/                  # Claude Code skill definitions\n        └── seo-audit/\n            └── SKILL.md\n```\n\n## Execution Flow (`run.py`)\n`run.py` acts as a headless orchestrator for the full pipeline. It executes the following sequence via the `server` module:\n\n1.  **`start_dashboard()`**: (Optional) Launches the HTTP/SSE server for real-time monitoring.\n2.  **`seo_load(export_dir)`**: Ingests the `internal_all.csv` from the Screaming Frog export.\n3.  **`seo_detect()`**: Runs deterministic detectors against the loaded data.\n4.  **`seo_recommend(recs)`**: Attaches starter recommendations (prioritizes top 5 issues).\n5.  **`seo_report()`**: Generates and saves `outputs/report.json`.\n6.  **`seo_export()`**: Renders and saves `outputs/report.html`.\n\n## Agent Responsibilities\nThe system uses a multi-agent architecture to move from raw detection to actionable fixes:\n\n| Agent | Responsibility | Primary Action |\n| :--- | :--- | :--- |\n| **Ingest** | Data loading and cleaning | Calls `seo_load` |\n| **Auditor** | Prioritization and impact analysis | Analyzes results of `seo_detect` |\n| **Fixer** | Generates model-driven fixes (Titles, Metas) | Calls `seo_set_fixes` |\n| **Reporter** | Final synthesis and report formatting | Calls `seo_report` & `seo_export` |\n\n## MCP Server Responsibilities (`mcp/server.py`)\nThe MCP server serves as the \"Brain\" of the system, providing both a tool-based API for agents and a real-time API for the dashboard.\n\n- **State Management**: Maintains a global `RUN` dictionary containing the current site, URLs, detected issues, fixes, and metadata.\n- **Tool Exposure**: Exposes the following tools to Claude Code:\n    - `load`: Load export directory.\n    - `detect_issues`: Run rulebook detectors.\n    - `set_fixes`: Attach AI-generated title/redirect fixes.\n    - `recommend`: Attach prioritized recommendations.\n    - `write_report`: Save JSON output.\n    - `export_report`: Save HTML output.\n- **Dashboard Hosting**: Serves a static frontend and an SSE event stream.\n- **Event Emission**: Pushes state changes to the dashboard via an internal `_emit` mechanism.\n\n## Dashboard Event Flow\nThe dashboard uses Server-Sent Events (SSE) to update in real-time without polling:\n\n1.  **Connection**: Frontend connects to `/events`.\n2.  **Snapshot**: Server immediately sends a `snapshot` event with current `RUN` state.\n3.  **Events**: As the pipeline progresses, the server emits:\n    - `loaded`: Site and URL count.\n    - `issue`: Individual detected issue (allows the UI to \"stream\" issues).\n    - `summary`: Final counts by severity.\n    - `fixes`: Updated titles/redirects.\n    - `recommendations`: The priority list.\n    - `saved`/`exported`: Notification that files are ready.\n\n## Report Generation Flow\nReports are generated in two formats:\n\n1.  **`report.json`**:\n    - The `_report_obj()` function aggregates state from the `RUN` dictionary.\n    - The resulting object is validated against `report.schema.json` and written to disk.\n2.  **`report.html`**:\n    - The report object is passed to `_render_html`.\n    - A standalone HTML page is generated with embedded CSS for a professional client deliverable.\n\n## Detector Flow (`seo/detector.py`)\nThe detection process is deterministic and uses only standard Python (CSV) to ensure speed and reliability:\n\n1.  **`load_rows()`**: Reads `internal_all.csv` into a list of dictionaries.\n2.  **`detect()`**: \n    - Filters rows into subsets: `html` (Content-Type check) and `idx200` (Status 200 + Indexable).\n    - Applies specific rules (e.g., Missing Title, Duplicate Title, 4xx/5xx Errors).\n    - Collects affected URLs and counts per issue type.\n3.  **`summarize()`**: Aggregates the issues into a total count and a breakdown by severity (High, Medium, Low).\n\n## TODO Locations\n- **`seo-command-center/run.py`**: Line 12-13 — Implementation of model-driven fixes (title rewriting, redirect maps).\n- **`seo-command-center/seo/detector.py`**: Line 93 — Implementation of the remaining rulebook detectors (too short titles, missing metas, etc.).\n"}}],"usage":{"input_tokens":35561,"cache_creation_input_tokens":0,"cache_read_input_tokens":0,"output_tokens":1469,"server_tool_use":{"web_search_requests":0,"web_fetch_requests":0},"service_tier":"standard","cache_creation":{"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0},"inference_geo":"","iterations":[],"speed":"standard"},"stop_reason":"tool_use","stop_details":null},"type":"assistant","uuid":"1bcad5e1-45a0-4fb0-a081-9c13a2b3e598","timestamp":"2026-06-06T07:30:53.183Z","userType":"external","entrypoint":"cli","cwd":"C:\\Users\\bisht\\Forge-Claude Code\\forge-sprint-01-starter","sessionId":"ea4dc880-de80-4803-ac63-6885c9915dd9","version":"2.1.167","gitBranch":"HEAD"}

Currently Implemented Detectors\nThe current implementation includes a \"starter set\" of 7 deterministic detectors:\n\n| Issue Type | Logic | Severity |\n| :--- | :--- | :--- |\n| `missing_title` | `Title 1` is empty on indexable 200 pages | High |\n| `duplicate_title` | 2+ indexable URLs sharing the same `Title 1` | High |\n| `title_too_long` | `Title 1 Pixel Width` > 561 OR `Title 1 Length` > 60 | Medium |\n| `broken_link` | `Status Code` between 400 and 499 | High |\n| `server_error` | `Status Code` between 500 and 599 | High |\n| `redirect` | `Status Code` between 300 and 399 | Medium |\n| `orphan_page` | `Inlinks` = 0 on indexable 200 pages | Medium |\n\n## 2. Available Helper Functions\nThe detector uses several utilities to handle the messy nature of CSV data:\n\n- **Data Loading**:\n    - `load_rows(export_dir)`: Loads `internal_all.csv` using `csv.DictReader`.\n- **Type Casting**:\n    - `_int(v, default=0)`: Safely converts strings to integers (handles floats and whitespace).\n    - `_float(v, default=0.0)`: Safely converts strings to floats.\n- **Filtering**:\n    - `is_html(r)`: Checks if the `Content Type` contains `text/html`.\n    - `is_200(r)`: Validates if the `Status Code` is exactly 200.\n    - `indexable(r)`: Validates if the `Indexability` column is exactly \"Indexable\".\n- **Aggregation**:\n    - `summarize(issues)`: Counts total issues and breaks them down by severity (`High`, `Medium`, `Low`).\n\n## 3. Missing Detectors (from `rulebook.md`)\nThe following rules are defined in the rulebook but not yet implemented in `detector.py`:\n\n- **Titles/Metas**: `title_too_short`, `missing_meta_description`, `duplicate_meta_description`, `meta_description_too_long`.\n- **Headers**: `missing_h1`, `duplicate_h1`.\n- **Links/Redirects**: `redirect_chain`.\n- **Content/Performance**: `thin_content`, `non_indexable_but_linked`, `slow_page`.\n\n## 4. Current Detection Limitations\n- **No Relational Analysis**: The current logic processes rows independently or via simple grouping. It cannot detect `redirect_chain` because that requires building a map of redirects and tracing the path.\n- **Partial Rulebook Coverage**: Only ~40% of the required rules are implemented.\n- **Basic Filtering**: While it has `idx200` and `html` filters, it does not yet implement more complex combined filters for all rule types (e.g., some rules might apply to all 200s, others only to indexable ones).\n\n## 5. Sample Export Reporting\nIf the sample export only reports 4 issue types despite 7 being implemented, it is because the **sample data specifically only contains those 4 types of errors**. The `detector.py` only adds an issue to the list if `urls` is non-empty (Line 50). Therefore, the output is a direct reflection of the flaws present in the `internal_all.csv` provided in the sample.\n\n## Recommended Implementation Order\n\nI recommend implementing the missing detectors in three waves to manage complexity:\n\n### Wave 1: Simple Column Checks (Quick Wins)\nThese only require a single `if` statement over a column for the `idx200` or `html` sets.\n1. `title_too_short`\n2. `missing_meta_description`\n3. `meta_description_too_long`\n4. `missing_h1`\n5. `thin_content`\n6. `slow_page`\n7. `non_indexable_but_linked`\n\n### Wave 2: Grouping/Deduplication\nThese require using `defaultdict` to find duplicates, similar to the existing `duplicate_title` logic.\n1. `duplicate_meta_description`\n2. `duplicate_h1`\n\n### Wave 3: Graph/Map Logic (High Complexity)\nThis requires building a state map of the entire crawl before detection.\n1. `redirect_chain` (Build `{Address: RedirectURL}` map $\\rightarrow$ trace targets)\n"}}],"usage":{"input_tokens":38138,"cache_creation_input_tokens":0,"cache_read_input_tokens":0,"output_tokens":1967,"server_tool_use":{"web_search_requests":0,"web_fetch_requests":0},"service_tier":"standard","cache_creation":{"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0},"inference_geo":"","iterations":[],"speed":"standard"},"stop_reason":"tool_use","stop_details":null},"type":"assistant","uuid":"68a104bb-53a1-465a-a671-f78161dfa86e","timestamp":"2026-06-06T07:41:09.042Z","userType":"external","entrypoint":"cli","cwd":"C:\\Users\\bisht\\Forge-Claude Code\\forge-sprint-01-starter","sessionId":"ea4dc880-de80-4803-ac63-6885c9915dd9","version":"2.1.167","gitBranch":"HEAD","slug":"eventual-floating-sky"}
